  <script type="text/javascript">
      function toggleTradeRouteBoxContent() {
          if ($('#tradeRouteBox').hasClass('hidden')) {
              $('#tradeRouteBox').removeClass('hidden');
              setCookie('hideTradeRouteBoxContent', 0, 5 * 365);
          } else {
              $('#tradeRouteBox').addClass('hidden');
              setCookie('hideTradeRouteBoxContent', 1, 5 * 365);
          }
      }
      function confirmTradeRouteDelete(link) {
          ikariam.createPopup("abortPopup", '',
              ['Desejas realmente apagar esta rota comercial? Podes simplesmente colocar os valores de comércio a 0.', link,
                  'Sim', 'Abortar'], 1);
      }
  
      function confirmTradeRouteActivate(number) {
  
          ikariam.createPopup("confirmPopup" + number, '',
              ['Completar a compra desta funcionalidade premium por 15 <img width=\"16\" height=\"20\" class=\"no_style vertical_middle\" alt=\"Ambrósia\" src=\"//gf2.geo.gfsrv.net/cdn43/4fdf6de0096451f0fb3e2cc18d8418.png\"> Ambrosia?',
                  ['$(\'#renew' + number + '\')[0].value=1;$(\'#tradeRouteForm' + number + '\').submit();return false;'],
                  'Sim', 'Abortar'], 1);
  
      }
  
  </script>

              <script type="text/javascript">
                  function setTradeRouteData() {
                      var number = 0;
                      var tradegood = 0;
                      var countGoods = 0;
  
                                          if ($('#textfield_wood')[0].value > number) {
                          number = $('#textfield_wood')[0].value;
                          tradegood = 0;
                          countGoods++;
                      }
                                          if ($('#textfield_wine')[0].value > number) {
                          number = $('#textfield_wine')[0].value;
                          tradegood = 1;
                          countGoods++;
                      }
                                          if ($('#textfield_marble')[0].value > number) {
                          number = $('#textfield_marble')[0].value;
                          tradegood = 2;
                          countGoods++;
                      }
                                          if ($('#textfield_glass')[0].value > number) {
                          number = $('#textfield_glass')[0].value;
                          tradegood = 3;
                          countGoods++;
                      }
                                          if ($('#textfield_sulfur')[0].value > number) {
                          number = $('#textfield_sulfur')[0].value;
                          tradegood = 4;
                          countGoods++;
                      }
                                          $('#tradeRouteNumber')[0].value = number;
                      $('#tradeRouteTradegood')[0].value = tradegood;
  
                      if (countGoods > 1) {
                          BubbleTips.bindBubbleTip(5, 11, 'Só podes estabelecer uma rota comercial com um tipo de mercadoria. Por favor coloca as restantes mercadorias a 0.');
                          return false;
                      }
                      return true;
                  }
              </script>
          <script type="text/javascript">
      // user input: premium ships' slider, resource sliders and buttons, price, draft, triton, freighters
      // game input: config values and defaults for that destination / mission
      // output: user input + actually used ships + estimated durations, premium costs
      // this is used for transport, buy, sell and blackMarket variants of that
  
      /*
       *  the controller objects
       *  jahrzehnte alter code... es geht eigentlich nur darum, die settings auf den transportscreens (transport, colonize und takeOffer) zu überwachen
       *  (sliderwerte, ambrosiakosten etc). dafür ist dieser riesen overload nicht notwendig. refactoring erwünscht...
       **/
      function transportETAController(config) {
          var journeyDuration = config.journeyDuration;
          var loadingSpeed = config.loadingSpeed;
          var queueTime = config.queueTime;
          var needsLoading = config.needsLoading;
          var wood = 0;
          var wine = 0;
          var crystal = 0;
          var sulfur = 0;
          var marble = 0;
          var gold = 0;
          var that = this;
          this.eta = journeyDuration;
          this.createEvent("ETAchanged");
  
          this.updatewood = function (res) {
              if (transportConfig.missionName === 'colonize') {
                  wood = parseInt(res) + transportConfig.COLONIZATION_MINIMUM_RESOURCE
                      + transportConfig.COLONIZATION_INITIAL_CITIZENS;
              } else {
                  wood = parseInt(res);
              }
              that.recalcETA();
          }
  
          this.updateglass = function (res) {
              crystal = parseInt(res);
              that.recalcETA();
          }
  
          this.updatewine = function (res) {
              wine = parseInt(res);
              that.recalcETA();
          }
  
          this.updatemarble = function (res) {
              marble = parseInt(res);
              that.recalcETA();
          }
  
          this.updatesulfur = function (res) {
              sulfur = parseInt(res);
              that.recalcETA();
          }
  
          this.updategold = function (res) {
              gold = parseInt(res);
              that.recalcETA();
          }
  
  
          this.updateJD = function (duration) {
              journeyDuration = duration;
              that.recalcETA();
          }
  
          this.recalcETA = function () {
              var res = wood + wine + crystal + marble + sulfur;
              this.eta = Math.ceil(Number(queueTime)) + Math.ceil(Number(journeyDuration));
  
              if (needsLoading === 1) {
                  var isSellOffer = transportConfig.viewOffersOfType && transportConfig.viewOffersOfType !== transportConfig.BUY_OFFER;
                  var loadingTimeResources = Number(res) / Number(loadingSpeed);
                  var loadingTimeGold = (Number(gold) / 25) / Number(loadingSpeed);
  
                  if (!config.isGoldPlunderingAllowed) {
                      loadingTimeGold = 0;
                  }
  
                  if (isSellOffer && !config.isMilitaryOffer) {
                      loadingTimeResources = 0;
                  }
  
                  var loadingTime = Math.ceil(Math.max(loadingTimeGold, loadingTimeResources));
                  this.eta += loadingTime;
  
                  if (loadingTime > 0) {
                      $('#loadingTime').html(ikariam.getTimestring(Number(loadingTime) * 1000, 3));
                  } else {
                      $('#loadingTime').html('-');
                  }
              }
  
              this.fireEvent("ETAchanged", Number(this.eta));
          }
      }
  
      /**
       * We needed to add a new controller to calculate the journey duration for
       * the draft feature (Tiefgang). Unfortunately the journeyDurationController
       * can only work with a list of inputs where each input represents a ship
       * type and has its own immutable duration. But since draft only works with
       * transporters we need something more flexible.
       *
       * Hence, journeyDraftController (the name sux, I know) takes the
       * capacityController to determine the current transporter speed.
       *
       * The new duration is determined by dividing the base speed by the new speed
       * and multiplying the result with the base duration. Idea behind this is:
       * If you drive From A to B at 100km/h in 60min you need only 30min if you
       * increase the speed to 200km/h. Hence:
       * -> 2*Speed => Time/2
       * -> NewSpeed = NewSpeedFactor*BaseSpeed => Time/NewSpeedFactor = Time * 1/NewSpeedfactor
       * -> NewSpeedfactor = NewSpeed/BaseSpeed
       * -> 1/NewSpeedFactor = BaseSpeed/NewSpeed
       */
      function journeyDraftDurationController(config) {
          var that = this;
          var baseJourneyDuration = config.journeyDuration;
          var baseTransporterSpeed = config.transporterSpeed;
          var poseidonEffect = config.poseidonEffect;
          var tritonInjectorLevel = config.tritonInjectorLevel;
          var fleetJourneyTime = config.fleetJourneyTime;
          var distance = config.distance;
          var marineChartArchiveBonus = config.marineChartArchiveBonus;
          var governmentBonus = config.governmentBonus;
  
          this.journeyDuration = baseJourneyDuration;
          this.transporterSpeed = baseTransporterSpeed;
          this.tritonInjectorLevel = tritonInjectorLevel;
          this.marineChartArchiveBonus = marineChartArchiveBonus;
          this.worldBonus = config.worldBonus;
          this.minimumJourneyDuration = config.minimumJourneyDuration;
  
          this.createEvent('journeyDurationChanged');
  
          this.updateTransporterSpeed = function (speed) {
              this.transporterSpeed = speed;
              that.recalcJourneyDuration();
          }
  
          this.updateTritonInjector = function (level) {
              this.tritonInjectorLevel = level;
              that.recalcJourneyDuration();
          }
  
          this.recalcJourneyDuration = function () {
              var fleetSpeed =
                  parseInt(this.transporterSpeed)
                  * parseFloat(this.worldBonus)
                  * parseFloat(governmentBonus)
                  * (1.0 + parseInt(this.tritonInjectorLevel)
                  + parseFloat(poseidonEffect));
  
              var uncappedDuration = Math.ceil(
                  ((distance * parseInt(fleetJourneyTime)) / fleetSpeed) * this.marineChartArchiveBonus
              );
              var calculatedDuration =
                  uncappedDuration > this.minimumJourneyDuration ? uncappedDuration : this.minimumJourneyDuration;
  
              if (transporterDraft.freighters > 0 && transporterCount.selectedFreighters > 0) {
                  // FREIGHTER_SHIP_BASE_SPEED_FACTOR == 20
                  this.journeyDuration = calculatedDuration * 20;
              } else {
                  this.journeyDuration = calculatedDuration;
              }
              $('#freightersCount').val(transporterCount.usedFreighters);
              $('#use_freighter_ships').val(transporterCount.usedFreighters);
              $('#totalFreighters').html(transporterCount.selectedFreighters);
              $('#journeyTime').html(ikariam.getTimestring(this.journeyDuration * 1000, 3));
              this.fireEvent('journeyDurationChanged', this.journeyDuration);
          }
      }
      /**
       * This is the main controller for the draft feature set (Tiefgang).
       * It holds capacity per transport and the resulting speed of the
       * transporter and informs others via custom events about changes to
       * these values.
       *
       * In order for this to work we need to register a single input
       * element that holds the available options and the corresponding
       * capacity and speed values.Implemented is registering a select
       * dropdown with options that hold the capacity as value and the
       * corresponding speed as an additional attribute.
       *
       * Example:
       * <select id="capacityPerTransport" name="capacityPerTransport">
       * <option value="$CAPACITY" speed="$SPEED">$CAPACITY</option>
       * </select>
       */
      function transporterDraftController(config) {
  
          // initial values
          var that = this;
          this.capacityPerTransport = 5; // starting value = 5 of 5 * 20% -> 100%, no speedup
          this.transporterSpeed = config.transporterSpeed;
          this.governmentBonus = config.governmentBonus;
          this.tritonInjectorLevel = config.tritonInjectorLevel;
          this.input = null;
          this.tritonInput = null;
          this.freighters = config.freighters;
  
          // custom events
          this.createEvent("capacityPerTransportChanged");
          this.createEvent("transporterSpeedChanged");
          this.createEvent("tritonChanged");
          this.createEvent("freighterChanged");
  
          // call if a change ist detected
          this.updateDraftParameters = function () {
              this.fireEvent("capacityPerTransportChanged", this.capacityPerTransport);
              this.fireEvent("transporterSpeedChanged", this.transporterSpeed);
              this.fireEvent("tritonChanged", this.tritonInjectorLevel);
              this.fireEvent("freighterChanged", this.freighters);
          };
  
          this.registerTritonInput = function (tritonInput) {
              this.tritonInput = tritonInput;
              $('#' + this.tritonInput).on('change', function () {
                  that.updateDraftParameters();
              });
          }
  
          this.setCapacityByDraft = function (capacity) {
              this.capacityPerTransport = capacity;
              that.updateDraftParameters();
          }
  
          this.setSpeed = function (speed) {
              this.transporterSpeed = parseInt(speed);
              that.updateDraftParameters();
          }
  
          this.setParametersFromDraftSlider = function (capacitySliderValue, speed) {
              this.capacityPerTransport = capacitySliderValue;
              this.transporterSpeed = speed;
              that.updateDraftParameters();
          }
  
          this.setFreighters = function (shipsCount) {
              this.freighters = shipsCount;
              that.updateDraftParameters();
          }
      }
  
      function transportController(config) {
          var that = this;
          var rI = [];
          var blockEvents = false;
          this.availableTransporters = config.availableTransporters;
          this.premiumTransporters = 0;
          this.capacityPerTransport = config.maxCapacityPerTransport; // beware: same name as in draft controller, but real capacity
          this.minimumResource = config.colonizationMinimumResource;
          this.spaceReserved = (typeof(config.spaceReserved) == 'undefined') ? 0 : config.spaceReserved;
          this.minimalNumberOfTransporters =
              (!(config.minimalNumberOfTransporters) || typeof(config.minimalNumberOfTransporters) == 'undefined') ? 0 :
                  parseInt(config.minimalNumberOfTransporters);
  
          this.totalCapacity = (config.useSmQ) ?
              (Math.min(config.haveSmQ, (this.availableTransporters * this.capacityPerTransport))) :
              (this.availableTransporters * this.capacityPerTransport); // initial value with 0 freighters
  
          this.usedCapacity = this.spaceReserved;
          this.remainingCapacity = this.totalCapacity - this.usedCapacity;
          this.usedTransporters = 0;
          this.registerSlider = this.registerInput;
          this.createEvent("usedTransChanged");
          this.createEvent("availTransChanged");
          this.usedCapacityRealWeight = 0;
          this.resourcesMax = [];
          this.loadingSpeed = config.loadingSpeed;
          this.isGoldPlunderingAllowed = config.isGoldPlunderingAllowed;
          this.queueTime = config.queueTime;
          this.journeyDuration = config.journeyDuration;
          this.freighters = config.freeFreighters;
          this.selectedFreighters = 0;
          this.usedFreighters = 0;
          this.capacityPerFreighter = transportConfig.freighterCapacity; // default: no draft yet
  
          this.registerInput = function (input, name, weight, realWeight, currency, price, updateTransporters) {
  
              if (typeof weight === 'undefined') weight = 1;
              weight = parseInt(weight);
  
              if (typeof realWeight === 'undefined') realWeight = 0;
              realWeight = parseInt(realWeight);
  
              if (typeof updateTransporters === 'undefined') updateTransporters = true;
  
              currency = parseInt(currency);
  
              price = parseInt(price);
  
              rI.push({
                  'input': input,
                  'name': name,
                  'currency': currency,
                  'weight': weight,
                  'realWeight': realWeight,
                  'oldMax': input.range[1],
                  'price': price,
                  'updateTransporters': updateTransporters
              });
              input.subscribe("change", function (e) {
                  that.realignInput()
              }, this, true);
              this.realignInput();
  
          };
  
          this.setPremiumTransporters = function (newValue) {
              var diff = newValue - this.premiumTransporters;
              this.premiumTransporters = newValue;
              this.setTransporters(this.availableTransporters + diff);
              this.updateCapacityDisplays('premium');
          };
          this.setNormalTransporters = function (newValue) {
              // available transporters contain the premium transporters, we only want to modify the other part
              var diff = newValue - (this.availableTransporters - this.premiumTransporters);
              this.setTransporters(this.availableTransporters + diff);
              this.updateCapacityDisplays('normal');
          }
  
          this.setTransporters = function (n) { // should only be called by setNormalTransporters + setPremiumTransporters
              this.availableTransporters = n;
              this.totalCapacity =
                  this.availableTransporters * this.capacityPerTransport
                  + this.selectedFreighters * this.capacityPerFreighter;
              this.totalCapacity = (config.useSmQ) ? Math.min(config.haveSmQ, this.totalCapacity) : this.totalCapacity;
  
              this.remainingCapacity = this.totalCapacity - Math.max(this.usedCapacity, this.usedCapacityRealWeight);
  
              if (this.remainingCapacity < 0) {
                  this.fixRemainingCapacity();
              }
              this.fireEvent(
                  'availTransChanged', // updates html only
                  { normal: this.availableTransporters - this.premiumTransporters, premium: this.premiumTransporters }
              );
  
              this.realignInput();
          };
  
          this.fixRemainingCapacity = function()
          {
              blockEvents = true;  //else infinite recursion when setting input values
              var currentUsedCapacity = 0;
              var currentUsedCapacityRealWeight = 0;
              for (var i = rI.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                  var newMax = +Infinity;
                  if (rI[i].weight) {
                      var nexMaxAccordingToResources = Math.floor((this.totalCapacity - currentUsedCapacity) / rI[i].weight);
                      newMax = Math.min(newMax, nexMaxAccordingToResources);
                  }
                  if (rI[i].realWeight) {
                      var nexMaxAccordingToWeight = Math.floor((this.totalCapacity - currentUsedCapacityRealWeight) / rI[i].realWeight);
                      newMax = Math.min(newMax, nexMaxAccordingToWeight);
                  }
                  var currentValue = parseInt(rI[i].input.input.value);
                  if (newMax < currentValue) { // does not fit in
                      currentValue = newMax;
                      rI[i].input.setRange([0, currentValue]);
                      rI[i].input.setValue(currentValue)
                      if (transportConfig.summaryIncluded) {
                          $('#' + rI[i].input.input.id.replace('textfield_', 'summary_'))
                              .val(currentValue)
                      }
                  }
                  currentUsedCapacity += currentValue * rI[i].weight;
                  currentUsedCapacityRealWeight += currentValue * rI[i].realWeight;
              }
              this.usedCapacity = currentUsedCapacity;
              this.usedCapacityRealWeight = currentUsedCapacityRealWeight;
              this.remainingCapacity = this.totalCapacity - Math.max(this.usedCapacity, this.usedCapacityRealWeight);
              blockEvents = false;  //all fine
          }
  
          this.setResources = function (resources) {
              this.resourcesMax = resources;
              this.resourcesInUse = [0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0];
          };
  
          this.setMax = function (elementName) {
              for (var i = rI.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                  if (rI[i].name === elementName) {
                      rI[i].input.setValue(rI[i].input.range[1]);
                      this.realignInput();
                  }
              }
  
          };
  
          this.setPrice = function (elementName, newPrice) {
              if (newPrice < 0) return false;
              for (var i = rI.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                  if (rI[i].name === elementName) {
                      var currentValue = parseInt(rI[i].input.input.value);
                      var alreadySelectedResources = currentValue * rI[i].price;
                      var additionalResourcesAvailable = this.resourcesMax[rI[i].currency] - this.resourcesInUse[rI[i].currency];
                      var sum = alreadySelectedResources + additionalResourcesAvailable;
                      var purchasableWithNewPrice = Math.min(currentValue, Math.floor(sum / newPrice)); // no automatic increase
  
                      var enoughCapacity = true;
                      if (rI[i].weight > 0) {
                          var maximumForCapacity =
                              this.totalCapacity - this.usedCapacityResource + currentValue * rI[i].weight;
                          if (currentValue * newPrice > maximumForCapacity) {
                              // we are only changing the price here, so there is no need to check the realWeight
                              enoughCapacity = false;
                          }
                      }
  
                      if (newPrice <= rI[i].price || (purchasableWithNewPrice >= currentValue && enoughCapacity)) {
  
                          if (rI[i].weight > 0 && rI[i].currency !== 5) { // 5: gold
                              rI[i].weight = newPrice;
                          }
                          rI[i].price = newPrice;
                          this.realignInput();
                          return rI[i].price;
                      } else {
                          return rI[i].price;
                      }
                  }
              }
              return false;
          };
  
          this.realignInput = function () {
              if (blockEvents) return false;
              this.usedCapacity = this.spaceReserved;
              this.usedCapacityRealWeight = 0;
              this.resourcesInUse = [0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0];
              for (var i = rI.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                  var currentValue1 = parseInt(rI[i].input.input.value);
                  this.usedCapacity += currentValue1 * rI[i].weight;
                  this.usedCapacityRealWeight += currentValue1 * rI[i].realWeight;
                  if (transportConfig.viewOffersOfType === transportConfig.BUY_OFFER) {
                      this.resourcesInUse[i] += currentValue1 * rI[i].weight;
                  } else if (rI[i].currency !== 5) { // 5: gold
                      this.resourcesInUse[rI[i].currency] += currentValue1 * rI[i].weight;
                  } else {
                      this.resourcesInUse[5] += currentValue1 * rI[i].price;
                  }
              }
  
              this.usedCapacityResource = this.usedCapacity;
              this.usedCapacity = Math.max(this.usedCapacity, this.usedCapacityRealWeight)
  
              if (this.minimalNumberOfTransporters > 0 && this.usedCapacity === 0) {
                  this.usedCapacity += this.minimalNumberOfTransporters * this.capacityPerTransport;
                  // colonization: 3 transporters for 1250 wood are always required.
                  // black market: even for war ships there always needs to be one full transporter involved
              }
              this.remainingCapacity = Math.max(0, this.totalCapacity - this.usedCapacity);
  
              this.usedFreighters = Math.min(
                  Math.ceil(this.saveDivide(this.usedCapacity, this.capacityPerFreighter)),
                  this.selectedFreighters // do not use more than the selected freighters
              );
              var neededTransporters = Math.ceil(this.saveDivide(
                  Math.max(
                      0, // do not use negative transporters for the unused capacity in a freighter not completely filled
                      this.usedCapacity - this.usedFreighters * this.capacityPerFreighter
                  ),
                  this.capacityPerTransport
              ));
  
              var usedPremiumTransporters = Math.max(0, Math.min(neededTransporters, this.premiumTransporters));
              this.usedTransporters = Math.max(0, neededTransporters - usedPremiumTransporters);
  
              ambrosiaTransporter = getPremiumTransporterCosts(usedPremiumTransporters);
              this.fireEvent("freighterChanged", this.usedFreighters);
              this.fireEvent(
                  'usedTransChanged',
                  {
                      normal: Math.min(this.usedTransporters, this.availableTransporters - this.premiumTransporters),
                      premium: usedPremiumTransporters
                  }
              );
              journeyDurationTriton.recalcJourneyDuration();
  
              if (transportConfig.missionName === 'trade') {
                  for (var i = rI.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                      var currentValue = parseInt(rI[i].input.input.value);
                      var maxCapacity, maxCapacityRealWeight, maxFromCurrency;
                      if (rI[i].weight > 0) {
                          maxCapacity = Math.max(
                              0,
                              Math.floor(
                                  (
                                      (this.totalCapacity - this.usedCapacityResource)
                                      + currentValue * rI[i].weight)
                                  / rI[i].weight)
                          );
                      } else {
                          maxCapacity = rI[i].oldMax;
                      }
                      if (rI[i].realWeight > 0) {
                          maxCapacityRealWeight = Math.max(
                              0,
                              Math.floor(
                                  (
                                      (this.totalCapacity - this.usedCapacityRealWeight)
                                      + currentValue * rI[i].realWeight)
                                  / rI[i].realWeight)
                          );
                      } else {
                          maxCapacityRealWeight = rI[i].oldMax;
                      }
  
                      if (rI[i].currency != 5) {
                          maxFromCurrency = Math.floor(
                              currentValue
                              + ((this.resourcesMax[rI[i].currency] - this.resourcesInUse[rI[i].currency])
                                  / rI[i].weight));
                      } else {
  
                          maxFromCurrency = Math.floor(
                              currentValue
                              + ((this.resourcesMax[5] - this.resourcesInUse[5]) / rI[i].price));
                      }
  
                      var maxRange = Math.max(
                          currentValue,
                          Math.min(
                              maxFromCurrency,
                              rI[i].oldMax,
                              maxCapacity,
                              maxCapacityRealWeight
                          )
                      );
                      rI[i].input.setRange([0, maxRange]);
                      rI[i].input.checkValue(currentValue);
                  }
              } else {
                  for (var j = rI.length - 1; j >= 0; j--) {
                      rI[j].input.setRange([0, Math.min(rI[j].oldMax, this.remainingCapacity + parseInt(rI[j].input.value))]);
                  }
              }
  
              this.updateCapacityDisplays('freighters');
          }
  
          /* changes the used capacity per transporter */
          this.setCapacityByDraft = function (capacitySliderValue) {
              this.capacityPerTransport = transportConfig.maxCapacityPerTransport * capacitySliderValue / 5;
              this.capacityPerFreighter = transportConfig.freighterCapacity * capacitySliderValue / 5;
              this.totalCapacity = this.availableTransporters * this.capacityPerTransport
                  + this.selectedFreighters * this.capacityPerFreighter;
              this.totalCapacity = (config.useSmQ) ? Math.min(config.haveSmQ, this.totalCapacity) : this.totalCapacity;
              if (this.totalCapacity < this.usedCapacity) {
                  this.fixRemainingCapacity();
              }
              this.updateCapacityDisplays('premium');
              this.updateCapacityDisplays('normal');
              this.updateCapacityDisplays('freighters');
              this.realignInput();
          }
  
          this.saveDivide = function (a, b) {
              return (b !== 0) ? a / b : 0;
          }
          this.updateJourneyDuration = function (duration) {
              this.journeyDuration = duration;
          }
          this.setSelectedFreighters = function (shipsCount) {
              this.selectedFreighters = shipsCount;
              transporterDraft.updateDraftParameters();
          }
  
          this.updateCapacityDisplays = function (target) {
              if (target === 'premium') {
                  $('.js_premiumTransportersCapacity').html('+ ' + ikariam.model.shortenValue(
                      this.premiumTransporters * this.capacityPerTransport, 5
                  ));
              } else if (target === 'normal') {
                  $('.js_transportersCapacity').html('+ ' + ikariam.model.shortenValue(
                      (this.availableTransporters - this.premiumTransporters) * this.capacityPerTransport, 5
                  ));
              } else if (target === 'freighters') {
                  $('.js_freightersCapacity').html(
                      '+ ' + ikariam.model.shortenValue(this.selectedFreighters * this.capacityPerFreighter, 5
                  ));
              }
              $('.js_completeTransportCapacity span').html(
                  ikariam.model.shortenValue(
                      this.availableTransporters * this.capacityPerTransport
                      + this.selectedFreighters * this.capacityPerFreighter,
                      5
                  )
              )
          }
      }
  
      transportController = $.extend(transportController, EventProvider);
      transporterDraftController = $.extend(transporterDraftController, EventProvider);
      transportETAController = $.extend(transportETAController, EventProvider);
      journeyDraftDurationController = $.extend(journeyDraftDurationController, EventProvider);
  
  
  
      function checkTransporterForm(ev) {
  
          if (ambrosiaTransporter + ambrosiaTriton > 0 && transportConfig.ambrosiaConfirmActive) {
              ikariam.getPopupController().createPopup(
                  'transportPopup',
                  '',
                  [
                      LocalizationStrings.transportConfig.securityQuestion1
                      + '<br><br>'
                      + LocalizationStrings.transportConfig.premiumTransportersName
                      + " (" + $('.premiumTransporterCount').val()
                      + ' ' + LocalizationStrings.transportConfig.ships + "):"
                      + '<br>'
                      +"<img src='/cdn/all/both/resources/icon_ambrosia_small.png' /> "
                      + ambrosiaTransporter + "<br>"
                      + LocalizationStrings.transportConfig.triton + ":"
                      + '<br>'
                      + "<img src='/cdn/all/both/resources/icon_ambrosia_small.png' /> "
                      + ambrosiaTriton,
                      ["ajaxHandlerCallFromForm($('#transportForm')[0]);"],
                      LocalizationStrings['yes'],
                      LocalizationStrings['abort']
                  ],
                  1
              );
          } else {
              ajaxHandlerCallFromForm($('#transportForm')[0]);
          }
      }

       *  and set up the required scripts on the screen (optional: triton, capacity, mission summary, premium transports)
       */

                  costs[374] = 16;
                  costs[375] = 16;
                  return costs[shipCount];
      }
  
      var ambrosiaTransporter = 0;
      var ambrosiaTriton = 0;
  
      /* init controller for capacity, duration and count */
      transporterCount = new transportController(transportConfig);
      transporterDraft = new transporterDraftController(transportConfig);
      etaControllerTriton = new transportETAController(transportConfig);
      journeyDurationTriton = new journeyDraftDurationController(transportConfig);
  
      if (transportConfig.premiumTransportsIncluded) {
          /* premium transporters */
          var premiumInput = new valueInput('textfield_premium', [0, transportConfig.avatarMaxTransporters]);
          var premiumSlider = new Slider('sliderthumb_premium', {
              'from': premiumInput,
              'dir': transportConfig.languageDirection
          });
          uiManager.connect(premiumSlider, premiumInput);
  
          $('#slider_premium_min').on('click', function (ev) {
              premiumSlider.setValue(premiumSlider.range[0]);
              $.stopEvent(ev);
          });
          $('#slider_premium_max').on('click', function (ev) {
              premiumSlider.setValue(premiumSlider.range[1]);
              $.stopEvent(ev);
          });
  
          $('.premiumTransporters .questionMark').on('click', function (e) {
              $('.js_premiumTransporterDescription').toggle();
              ikariam.getController().adjustSizes();
          });
  
          premiumSlider.subscribe('change', function (v) {
              transporterCount.setPremiumTransporters(v);
          });
      }
  
      if ($('#sliderthumb_transporters').length) {
          // normal transporters slider
          var normalTransportersInput = new valueInput(
              'selectedTransportersInput',
              [0, transportConfig.availableTransporters]
          );
          var normalTransporterSlider = new Slider(
              'sliderthumb_transporters',
              {'from': normalTransportersInput, 'dir': transportConfig.languageDirection}
          );
          uiManager.connect(normalTransporterSlider, normalTransportersInput);
  
          normalTransporterSlider.subscribe('change', function(newValue) {
              transporterCount.setNormalTransporters(newValue);
          });
  
          $('#slider_transporters_min').on('click', function (ev) {
              normalTransporterSlider.setValue(normalTransporterSlider.range[0]);
              $.stopEvent(ev);
          });
          $('#slider_transporters_max').on('click', function (ev) {
              normalTransporterSlider.setValue(normalTransporterSlider.range[1]);
              $.stopEvent(ev);
          });
      }
  
  
      for (var key = 0; key < transportConfig.currentCityTradeGoods.length; ++key) {
          var amount = transportConfig.currentCityTradeGoods[key];
          if (amount <= 0) {
              continue;
          }
          var currentResource = transportConfig.oldTradeGoodIdentifiers[key];
          if (transportConfig.maxCapacityOfNewCity[key] > 0) {
              if (key === 0) { // colonization + key wood
                  amount = Math.max(0, amount - transportConfig.COLONIZATION_MINIMUM_RESOURCE);
              }
              amount = Math.min(transportConfig.maxCapacityOfNewCity[key], amount);
          }
  
          window['i' + currentResource] =
              new valueInput('textfield_' + currentResource, [0, amount]);
          $('#textfield_' + currentResource).on('focus', function(event) {
              event.target.select();
          });
          if (transportConfig.summaryIncluded) {
              window['sum' + currentResource] =
                  new valueInput('summary_' + currentResource, [0, amount]);
          }
          window['s' + currentResource] = new Slider('sliderthumb_' + currentResource, {
              'from': window['i' + currentResource],
              'dir': transportConfig.LANGUAGE_DIRECTION
          });
          uiManager.connect(window['s' + currentResource], window['i' + currentResource]);
          if (transportConfig.summaryIncluded) {
              window['s' + currentResource].subscribe(
                  'change',
                  function (val) {
                      $(this)
                          .val(ikariam.model.shortenValue(val, 6))
                          .attr('title', ikariam.model.locaNumberFormat(val));
                  },
                  $('#summary_' + currentResource),
                  true
              );
          }
  
          $('#slider_' + currentResource + '_min')
              .on('click', { current: currentResource }, function (ev) {
                  window['s' + ev.data.current].setValue(window['s' + ev.data.current].range[0]);
                  $.stopEvent(ev);
              }
          );
          $('#slider_' + currentResource + '_max')
              .on('click', { current: currentResource }, function (ev) {
                  window['s' + ev.data.current].setValue(window['s' + ev.data.current].range[1]);
                  $.stopEvent(ev);
              }
          );
  
          if (!transportConfig.premiumColonization) { // no trade ships needed for premium colonization
              transporterCount.registerInput(window['s' + currentResource]);
          }
  
          etaControllerTriton['update' + currentResource](window['s' + currentResource].value);
          window['s' + currentResource].subscribe('change', function (val, data) {
              etaControllerTriton['update' + data.current](val);
          }, { current: currentResource });
      }
  
      if (transportConfig.tritonIncluded || transportConfig.capacityIncluded) {
          transporterDraft.registerTritonInput(0);
  
          /*
           * notify controllers on events
           */
          transporterDraft.subscribe('capacityPerTransportChanged', function (capacitySliderValue) {
              transporterCount.setCapacityByDraft(capacitySliderValue);
          });
          transporterDraft.subscribe('transporterSpeedChanged', function (speed) {
              journeyDurationTriton.updateTransporterSpeed(speed);
          });
          transporterDraft.subscribe('freighterChanged', function (ships) {
              ships = typeof ships === 'undefined' ? 0 : ships;
              transporterCount.usedFreighters = ships;
              transporterCount.realignInput();
          });
  
          /*
           * update gui on events
           */
          transporterCount.subscribe('usedTransChanged', function (data) {
              $('#transporterCount').val(data.normal);
              $('.premiumTransporterCount').val(data.premium);
  
              var $ambrosiaCostsDisplay = $('#ambrosiaCosts');
              var oldCosts = parseInt($ambrosiaCostsDisplay.html());
              var $premiumTransporterTextElem = $('#premiumTransporterText');
              if (ambrosiaTransporter > 0) {
                  if (transportConfig.ambrosia >= ambrosiaTransporter) {
                      $premiumTransporterTextElem.addClass("green").removeClass("red");
                      $('#ambrosiaWarningBox').addClass("invisible");
                  } else {
                      $premiumTransporterTextElem.addClass("red").removeClass("green");
                      $('#missingAmbrosia').html(ambrosiaTransporter - transportConfig.ambrosia);
                      $('#ambrosiaWarningBox').removeClass("invisible");
                  }
  
                  $ambrosiaCostsDisplay.html(ambrosiaTransporter);
                  $('.js_summaryPremiumTransporterAmbrosia').html(ambrosiaTransporter);
  
                  $('#js_tradeRouteButton').attr('disabled', true);
                  if (oldCosts === 0) {
                      $premiumTransporterTextElem.fadeIn();
                  }
              } else {
                  $premiumTransporterTextElem.removeClass("green").removeClass("red").fadeOut();
                  $('#ambrosiaWarningBox').addClass("invisible");
                  $ambrosiaCostsDisplay.html('0');
                  $('.js_summaryPremiumTransporterAmbrosia').html('0');
                  $('#js_tradeRouteButton').attr('disabled', this.selectedFreighters > 0);
              }
              $('#transportDisplayPrice').val(ambrosiaTriton + ambrosiaTransporter);
              $('.js_sumOfAmbrosiaCosts').html(ambrosiaTriton + ambrosiaTransporter);
          });
  
          transporterCount.subscribe('availTransChanged', function (data) {
              $('.totalNormalTransporters').html(data.normal);
              $('.totalPremiumTransporters').html(data.premium);
          });
  
          etaControllerTriton.subscribe('ETAchanged', function (eta) {
              $('#arrival').html(getFormattedDate(eta * 1000, transportConfig.DATETIME_FORMAT));
          });
          journeyDurationTriton.subscribe('journeyDurationChanged', function (duration) {
              if (transportConfig.missionName === 'trade') {
                  transporterCount.updateJourneyDuration(duration);
              }
              etaControllerTriton.updateJD(duration);
          });
      }
  
      if (transportConfig.tritonIncluded && transportConfig.PREMIUM_TRITON_ACTIVATED > 0) {
          /* jet propulsion slider */
          var jetInput = new valueInput('textfield_jet', [0, 3]); // max. +300% speed
          var jetSlider = new Slider('sliderthumb_jet', {'from': jetInput, 'dir': transportConfig.languageDirection});
          uiManager.connect(jetSlider, jetInput);
  
          $('#slider_jet_min').on('click', function (ev) {
              jetSlider.setValue(jetSlider.range[0]);
              $.stopEvent(ev);
          });
          $('#slider_jet_max').on('click', function (ev) {
              jetSlider.setValue(jetSlider.range[1]);
              $.stopEvent(ev);
          });
  
          $('#setPremiumJetPropulsion .questionMark').on('click', function () {
              $('.js_tritonDescription').toggle();
              ikariam.getController().adjustSizes();
          });
  
          jetSlider.subscribe('change', function (v) {
              var newSpeed = '+' + v * 100 + '%';
              $('#speedValue').html(newSpeed);
              if (transportConfig.summaryIncluded) {
                  $('#summary_triton').val(newSpeed);
              }
  
              var currentCapacitySpeed = 0;
              if (transportConfig.capacityIncluded) {
                  currentCapacitySpeed = Math.round(
                      (parseInt($('#max_capacity').val()) - parseInt($('#sliderbg_capacity').attr('title')))
                      * 16.6 * 10) / 10;
              }
              if (transportConfig.summaryIncluded) {
                  $('#summary_total').val('+' + (v * 100 + currentCapacitySpeed
                          + transportConfig.poseidonEffect * 100)
                      + '%');
              }
  
              var ambrosiaCosts = 0,
                  itemCosts;
  
              if (v > transportConfig.tritonItemCount) {
                  ambrosiaCosts = transportConfig.tritonPrice[v - transportConfig.tritonItemCount];
                  itemCosts = transportConfig.tritonItemCount;
              } else {
                  itemCosts = v;
              }
  
              $('#jetAmbrosiaCosts').html(ambrosiaCosts);
              $('#jetItemCosts').html(itemCosts);
              ambrosiaTriton = ambrosiaCosts;
              $('.js_summaryTritonCosts').html(ambrosiaTriton);
              $('.js_sumOfAmbrosiaCosts').html(ambrosiaTriton+ambrosiaTransporter);
              $('#transportDisplayPrice').val(ambrosiaTriton+ambrosiaTransporter);
              journeyDurationTriton.updateTritonInjector(v);
          });
      }
  
      if (transportConfig.capacityIncluded) {
          /* capacity slider */
          var capacityInput = new valueInput('textfield_capacity', [1, 5]); // - 80% .. - 0%
          var capacitySlider = new Slider('sliderthumb_capacity', {
              'from': capacityInput,
              'dir': transportConfig.languageDirection
          });
          uiManager.connect(capacitySlider, capacityInput);
  
          $('#max_capacity').val(capacitySlider.range[1]);
          capacitySlider.setValue(capacitySlider.range[1]);
  
          $('#slider_capacity_min').on('click', function (ev) {
              capacitySlider.setValue(capacitySlider.range[0]);
              $.stopEvent(ev);
          });
          $('#slider_capacity_max').on('click', function (ev) {
              capacitySlider.setValue(capacitySlider.range[1]);
              $.stopEvent(ev);
          });
          capacitySlider.subscribe('change', function (v) {
              v = parseInt(v);
              diffFromMax = capacitySlider.range[1] - v;
              roundedDiff = Math.round(diffFromMax * 16.666 * 10) / 10;// rounded to 1 digit
              capacityMalus = 100 - v * 20;
              $('#capacitySpeedValue').html('+' + roundedDiff + '%'); // basically it's 16,66666666...%
  
              $('.js_capacityModifier')
                  .html('-' + capacityMalus + '%')
                  .attr('title', LocalizationStrings.transportConfig.cargoSpace + ': '
                  + LocalizationStrings.transporter + ': '
                  + Math.round(transportConfig.maxCapacityPerTransport * v / 5) + ', '
                  + LocalizationStrings.freighter + ': '
                  + Math.round(transportConfig.freighterCapacity * v / 5)
              );
              if (transportConfig.summaryIncluded) {
                  $('#summary_capacity').val('+' + roundedDiff + '%');
                  if (transportConfig.PREMIUM_TRITON_ACTIVATED) {
                      $('#summary_total').val(
                          '+' + ($('#sliderbg_jet')[0].title * 100 + roundedDiff
                              + transportConfig.poseidonEffect * 100) + '%'
                      );
                  } else {
                      $('#summary_total').val('+' + (roundedDiff + transportConfig.poseidonEffect * 100) + '%');
                  }
              }
              transporterDraft.setParametersFromDraftSlider(v, transportConfig.transporterSpeed + diffFromMax * 10);
          });
      }
  
      if (transportConfig.summaryIncluded) {
          /**mission summary box*/
          $('#summary_wonder').val("+" + transportConfig.poseidonEffect * 100 + "%");
          $('#summary_total').val("+" + transportConfig.poseidonEffect * 100 + "%");
  
          $('#missionSummary').find('.pulldown').each(function () {
              $(this).children('.content').slideUp(0);
              $(this).children('.btn')
                  .on('mouseover',
                      function () {
                          $(this).css('background', 'url(/cdn/all/both/interface/pulldown_contentbox_hover.png)');
                      })
                  .on('mouseout',
                      function () {
                          $(this).css('background', 'url(/cdn/all/both/interface/pulldown_contentbox.png)');
                      })
                  .on('click',
                      function () {
                          $(this).prev().slideToggle({
                              duration: 100,
                              progress: function() { ikariam.getController().adjustSizes(); }
                          });
                      });
          });
      }
  
      if (transportConfig.tradeRoutesIncluded) {
          function setTradeRouteData() {
              var number = 0;
              var tradegood = 0;
              var countGoods = 0;
  
              for (var key = 0; key < transportConfig.currentCityTradeGoods.length; ++key) {
                  var amount = transportConfig.currentCityTradeGoods[key];
                  var currentResource = transportConfig.oldTradeGoodIdentifiers[key];
  
                  if (amount <= 0) {
                      continue;
                  }
                  var currentElem = $('#textfield_' + currentResource);
                  if (currentElem.val() > 0) {
                      number = currentElem.val();
                      tradegood = key;
                      countGoods++;
                  }
              }
  
              $('#tradeRouteNumber').val(number);
              $('#tradeRouteTradegood').val(tradegood);
              if (countGoods > 1) {
                  alert(LocalizationStrings.transportConfig.onlyOneTradeGood);
                  return false;
              }
              return true;
          }
      }
  
  
      // freighters should be available for transport, buy, sell
      if ($('#sliderthumb_freighters').length) {
          var inputFreighters = new valueInput('selectedFreightersInput', [0, transportConfig.freeFreighters]);
          var freightersSlider = new Slider('sliderthumb_freighters', {
              'from': inputFreighters,
              'dir': transportConfig.languageDirection
          });
          uiManager.connect(freightersSlider, inputFreighters);
          $('#slider_freighters_min').on('click', function (ev) {
              freightersSlider.setValue(freightersSlider.range[0]);
              $.stopEvent(ev);
          });
          $('#slider_freighters_max').on('click', function (ev) {
              freightersSlider.setValue(freightersSlider.range[1]);
              $.stopEvent(ev);
          });
          freightersSlider.subscribe('change', function (v) {
              $('#selectedFreightersInput').val(v);
              transporterDraft.setFreighters(v);
              transporterCount.setSelectedFreighters(v);
          });
      }
  
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
      function toggleTradeRouteBoxContent() {
          if ($('#tradeRouteBox').hasClass('hidden')) {
              $('#tradeRouteBox').removeClass('hidden');
              setCookie('hideTradeRouteBoxContent', 0, 5 * 365);
          } else {
              $('#tradeRouteBox').addClass('hidden');
              setCookie('hideTradeRouteBoxContent', 1, 5 * 365);
          }
      }
      function confirmTradeRouteDelete(link) {
          ikariam.createPopup("abortPopup", '',
              ['Desejas realmente apagar esta rota comercial? Podes simplesmente colocar os valores de comércio a 0.', link,
                  'Sim', 'Abortar'], 1);
      }
  
      function confirmTradeRouteActivate(number) {
  
          ikariam.createPopup("confirmPopup" + number, '',
              ['Completar a compra desta funcionalidade premium por 15 <img width=\"16\" height=\"20\" class=\"no_style vertical_middle\" alt=\"Ambrósia\" src=\"//gf2.geo.gfsrv.net/cdn43/4fdf6de0096451f0fb3e2cc18d8418.png\"> Ambrosia?',
                  ['$(\'#renew' + number + '\')[0].value=1;$(\'#tradeRouteForm' + number + '\').submit();return false;'],
                  'Sim', 'Abortar'], 1);
  
      }
  
  </script>

  <script>
      function checkCityIconForm(href, iconType) {
          var templateParams = ikariam.getTemplateData();
          var description = iconType > 0 ?  templateParams['cityIcons']['selectIconPopupQuestion'] :
              templateParams['cityIcons']['selectIconDefaultPopupQuestion']
           ikariam.getPopupController().createPopup(
              'cityIconPopup',
              '',
              [
                  description
                  + '<br><br>',
                  [`ajaxHandlerCall('${href}&resetAll=1');`, `ajaxHandlerCall('${href}&resetAll=0');`],
                  templateParams['cityIcons']['resetAll'],
                  templateParams['cityIcons']['resetCurrent']
              ],
              1
          );
      }
  </script>
